STAT table

STAT table

Info

Assistant ExtraLight Regular (Assistant-ExtraLight.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Info

Assistant Light Regular (Assistant-Light.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '

NID 6 is 'Assistant-ExtraLight', Everything looks good.

Assistant ExtraLight Regular (Assistant-ExtraLight.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Assistant' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraLight' = NID 1 'Assistant ExtraLight'.

Pass

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

NID 6 is 'Assistant-Light', Everything looks good.

Assistant Light Regular (Assistant-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Assistant' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Assistant Light'.

Pass

Assistant SemiBold Regular (Assistant-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Assistant-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Pass

Assistant SemiBold Regular (Assistant-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Assistant' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Assistant SemiBold'.

Pass

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

Assistant ExtraBold Regular (Assistant-ExtraBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Assistant' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraBold' = NID 1 'Assistant ExtraBold'.

Pass
